	<script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function(){
            $('#mobmenu_wrap .toggle').click(function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                var $this = $(this);

                if ($this.next().hasClass('show')) {
                    $this.closest('li.nav-link').removeClass('active');
                    $this.next().removeClass('show').slideUp(350);
                } else {
                    $this.parent().parent().find('li .inner').removeClass('show').slideUp(350);
                    $this.parent().parent().find('li.nav-link').removeClass('active');
                    $this.next().toggleClass('show').slideToggle(350);
                    $this.closest('li.nav-link').toggleClass('active');
                }
            });
        });
	</script>

class="fon-main-section clearfix row-heading-left row_mve6  " style=" "><div class="container "><div class="row justify-content-center " ><div id="col_ikm8la" class="col-12 col-sm-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3 Biz</h3></div></div><div id="fon-widget-text_html_ylhvnu" class="fon-widget-container fon-text-html-widget "><h3 class="fon-widget-title">Bizi Farklı Kılan <b>Nedir</b>?</h3><div class="fon-widget-content"><p>Sadece fiyat değil, sunduğumuz değer ile öne çıkıyor, müşterilerimize işlerini büyütmelerine yardımcı oluyoruz. </p></div></div></div><div id="col_vgqm" class="col-12 col-sm-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3 col-xl-3 col-heading-center   " data-aos="fade-up" data-aos-delay="100" data-aos-duration="600"  style=""><div id="fon-widget-feature_box_o2x0bw" class="fon-widget-container mb-0">Güvenli Altyapı ve Yedekleme</h6></div><div class="feature-box-content overflow-visible"><div class="feature-box-desc"><p>Verileriniz bizimle kale gibi korunur. En güncel güvenlik duvarları ve otomatik günlük yedekleme sistemleri sayesinde, siber tehditlere karşı tam koruma sağlarken veri kaybı riskini sıfıra indiriyoruz.
</p></div></div>
</div></div></div></div><div id="col_s9hw" class="col-12 col-sm-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3 col-xl-3 col-heading-center   " data-aos="fade-up" data-aos-delay="200" data-aos-duration="600"  style=""><div id="fon-widget-feature_box_ab7edz" class="fon-widget-container fon-feature-box-widget style-10 "><div class="fon-widget-content"><div class="feature-box overflow-visible h-100 flex-column media-left bg-white rounded-4 shadow-lg shadow-sm-hover"><div class="feature-box-media media-icon d-flex gap-3 mb-0 justify-content-start align-items-center text-start with-shadow border-bottom pb-3 "><div class="feature-box-media-container d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center rounded-3" style="width:40px; height:40px;"><i class="fa-solid fa-hand-holding-dollar feature-icon"></i></div><h6 class="feature-box-title fw-semibold mb-0">Şeffaf ve Uygun Fiyatlandırma</h6></div><div class="feature-box-content overflow-visible"><div class="feature-box-desc"><p>Sürpriz faturalara son veriyoruz. İhtiyacınıza en uygun paketi seçin, gizli ücretler olmadan sadece kullandığınız hizmetin bedelini ödeyin. Bütçe dostu, net ve anlaşılır fiyat politikamızla maliyetlerinizi yönetin </p></div></div>
</div></div></div></div><div id="col_fjra" class="col-12 col-sm-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3 col-xl-3 col-heading-center   " data-aos="fade-up" data-aos-delay="300" data-aos-duration="600"  style=""><div id="fon-widget-feature_box_cv2g" class="fon-widget-container fon-feature-box-widget style-10 "><div class="fon-widget-content"><div class="feature-box overflow-visible h-100 flex-column media-left bg-white rounded-4 shadow-lg shadow-sm-hover"><div class="feature-box-media media-icon d-flex gap-3 mb-0 justify-content-start align-items-center text-start with-shadow border-bottom pb-3 "><div class="feature-box-media-container d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center rounded-3" style="width:40px; height:40px;"><i class="fa-solid fa-rocket feature-icon"></i></div><h6 class="feature-box-title fw-semibold mb-0">Hızlı Kurulum Süreçleri</h6></div><div class="feature-box-content overflow-visible"><div class="feature-box-desc"><p>Projelerinizi hayata geçirmek için beklemeyin. Otomasyon sistemimiz sayesinde siparişinizin hemen ardından servisiniz aktif edilir. Zaman kaybetmeden işinize odaklanmanızı sağlıyoruz. </p></div></div>
</div></div></div></div><div id="col_nw7prw" class="col-12 col-sm-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3 col-xl-3 col-heading-center   " data-aos="fade-up" data-aos-delay="400" data-aos-duration="600"  style=""><div id="fon-widget-feature_box_qntfwe" class="fon-widget-container fon-feature-box-widget style-10 "><div class="fon-widget-content"><div class="feature-box overflow-visible h-100 flex-column media-left bg-white rounded-4 shadow-lg shadow-sm-hover"><div class="feature-box-media media-icon d-flex gap-3 mb-0 justify-content-start align-items-center text-start with-shadow border-bottom pb-3 "><div class="feature-box-media-container d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center rounded-3" style="width:40px; height:40px;"><i class="fa-solid fa-chart-area feature-icon"></i></div><h6 class="feature-box-title fw-semibold mb-0">Aylık Performans Raporları</h6></div><div class="feature-box-content overflow-visible"><div class="feature-box-desc"><p>Büyümenizi rakamlarla takip edin. Kaynak kullanımınızdan trafik analizlerine kadar detaylandırılmış aylık raporlarla sitenizin performansını şeffaf bir şekilde sunuyor, iyileştirme önerileri paylaşıyoruz. </p></div></div>
</div></div></div></div><div id="col_kcz8ww" class="col-12 col-sm-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3 col-xl-3 col-heading-center   " data-aos="fade-up" data-aos-delay="500" data-aos-duration="600"  style=""><div id="fon-widget-feature_box_is2zcg" class="fon-widget-container fon-feature-box-widget style-10 "><div class="fon-widget-content"><div class="feature-box overflow-visible h-100 flex-column media-left bg-white rounded-4 shadow-lg shadow-sm-hover"><div class="feature-box-media media-icon d-flex gap-3 mb-0 justify-content-start align-items-center text-start with-shadow border-bottom pb-3 "><div class="feature-box-media-container d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center rounded-3" style="width:40px; height:40px;"><i class="fa-solid fa-users feature-icon"></i></div><h6 class="feature-box-title fw-semibold mb-0">Genç ve Dinamik Ekip</h6></div><div class="feature-box-content overflow-visible"><div class="feature-box-desc"><p>Teknolojiyi takip eden değil, yön veren bir kadroyla çalışın. Enerjisi yüksek, yeniliklere açık uzman ekibimiz, işinize modern ve yaratıcı çözümler üretmek için sürekli kendini geliştiriyor. </p></div></div>

                    function newsletter_submit() {
                        var email = $("#newsletter_email input[name='email']").val();
			                                    MioAjaxElement($("#newsletter_submit"),{
                            waiting_text:"BEKLEYİNİZ",
                            result:"newsletter_result",

                    function newsletter_result(result) {
                        if(result != ''){
                            var solve = getJson(result);
                            if(solve !==false && solve != undefined && typeof(solve) == "object"){
                                if(solve.status == "error"){
                                    $("#newsletter_email input[name='email']").focus();
                                    swal({
                                        type: 'error',
                                        title: "Hata!",
                                        text: solve.message,
                                        timer: 2500,
                                        confirmButtonText: "Tamam",
                                    }).then(function () {
                                        $("#newsletter_email input[name='email']").focus();
                                    });
                                }else if(solve.status == "successful"){
                                    swal("Kaydedildi!", "Bülten aboneliğiniz kayıt edilmiştir.","success");
                                    $("#newsletter_email input[name='email']").val('');
                                }
                            }else
                                console.log(result);
                        }
                    }
                </script>
                        </div>
        </div>
    </div>

	<script>
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
            const header = document.getElementById("fon-header");
            const body = document.body;

            // Eğer header yoksa veya body'de sticky-header class'ı yoksa çalışmasın
            if (!header || !body.classList.contains('sticky-header')) return;

            // Hesaplamaları scroll dışında bir kere yapalım
            const headerOffset = header.offsetTop;
            const stickyPoint = headerOffset + 100;
            let ticking = false;

            window.addEventListener("scroll", function () {
                if (!ticking) {
                    window.requestAnimationFrame(function () {
                        // Scroll pozisyonunu al
                        const scrollTop = window.scrollY;

                        // Sadece durum değiştiğinde işlem yap (Performans Kilidi Burasıdır)
                        if (scrollTop >= stickyPoint) {
                            if (!header.classList.contains("header-fixed")) {
                                header.classList.add("header-fixed");
                            }
                        } else {
                            if (header.classList.contains("header-fixed")) {
                                header.classList.remove("header-fixed");
                            }
                        }

                        ticking = false;
                    });
                    ticking = true;
                }
            });
        });
	</script>

        <script>
            function formbuilder_gimcqu_submit(result){
                $('.captcha-img').each(function(){ var url = $(this).data('href') + '?time='+(new Date().getTime());$(this).attr('src',url); $(this).parent().next('input').val(''); });
                if(result != ""){
                    var solve = typeof result === "string" ? getJson(result) : result;
                    if(solve !==false && solve != undefined && typeof(solve) == "object"){                        
                        if(solve.status == "error"){
                            if(solve.for != undefined && solve.for != ""){
                                $("#fon-formbuilder_gimcqu").removeClass("was-validated");
                                $("#fon-formbuilder_gimcqu " +solve.for).focus();
                                $("#fon-formbuilder_gimcqu " +solve.for).addClass("is-invalid");
                                $("#fon-formbuilder_gimcqu " +solve.for).parent(".form-floating").addClass("is-invalid");
                                $("#fon-formbuilder_gimcqu " +solve.for).change(function(){
                                    $(this).removeClass("is-invalid");
                                     $(this).parent(".form-floating").removeClass("is-invalid");
                                });
                            }
                            if(solve.fors != undefined && solve.fors.length > 0){
                                $("#fonformbuilder_gimcqu").removeClass("was-validated");
                                for (var i = 0; i < solve.fors.length; i++) {
                                    $('#fon-formbuilder_gimcqu [name="formbuilder[' +solve.fors[i] + ']"]').addClass("is-invalid");
                                    $('#fon-formbuilder_gimcqu [name="formbuilder[' +solve.fors[i] + ']"]').parent(".form-floating").addClass("is-invalid");
                                    $('#fon-formbuilder_gimcqu [name="formbuilder[' +solve.fors[i] + ']"]').change(function(){
                                        $(this).removeClass("is-invalid");
                                        $(this).parent(".form-floating").removeClass("is-invalid");
                                    });
                                }
                            }
                            alert_error(solve.message,{timer:3000});
                        }
                        else if(solve.status == "success"){ 
                            alert_success(solve.message,{timer:3000});
                            setTimeout(function(){
                                location.reload();
                            }, 3000);
                        }
                    }else {
                        console.log(result);
                    }
                }
            }
            
            function initAllPhoneInputs() {
                if (typeof window.intlTelInput !== "function") {
                    return;
                }
                if (window.allPhonesInitialized) return;
            
                const telInputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[type="tel"]');
                if (telInputs.length === 0) {
                    return; 
                }
                
                const object_code = {
                    geoIpLookup: function (callback) {
                        callback("tr");
                    },
                    autoPlaceholder: "on",
                    formatOnDisplay: true,
                    initialCountry: "auto",                   
                    nationalMode: false,
                    placeholderNumberType: "MOBILE",
                    preferredCountries: ["tr","us", "gb", "ch", "ca", "de", "it"],
                    showSelectedDialCode: true,
                    countrySearch: true,
                    strictMode: true,
                    i18n: {
                        tr: "Türkiye",
                        searchPlaceholder: "Ara"
                    },
                    useFullscreenPopup: false,
                    utilsScript: "https://www.hostlar.com.tr/templates/website/Datawise/js/intltelinput/js/utils.js"
                };
                telInputs.forEach(function(input) {
                if (input.getAttribute("data-intl-initialized") === "true") return;
                
                input.setAttribute("data-intl-initialized", "true");
            
                const iti = window.intlTelInput(input, object_code);
                
                if (iti.promise) {
                    iti.promise.then(() => {
                        const hiddenInputId = input.id + "-hidden";
                        const hiddenInput = document.getElementById(hiddenInputId);
            
                        const updateHidden = () => {
                            if (hiddenInput) {
                                hiddenInput.value = iti.getNumber();
                            }
                        };
                            
                            updateHidden();
                            input.addEventListener("input", updateHidden);
                            input.addEventListener("countrychange", updateHidden);
                        });
                    }
                });
                window.allPhonesInitialized = true;
            }
            var phoneInitInterval = setInterval(function() {
                if (typeof window.intlTelInput === "function") {
                    initAllPhoneInputs();
                    if (window.allPhonesInitialized) {
                        clearInterval(phoneInitInterval);
                    }
                }
            }, 200);
            
            $(document).ready(function(){
                $("#fon-btn-formbuilder_gimcqu").on("click",function(e){
                    e.preventDefault();
                    var form = $("#fon-formbuilder_gimcqu");
                    if (!form[0].checkValidity()) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        form.addClass("was-validated");
                        form.find(":invalid").parent(".form-floating").addClass("is-invalid");
                        return (alert_error("Lütfen zorunlu tüm alanları doldurunuz.",{timer:3000}));
                    }
                    MioAjaxElement($(this),{
                        waiting_text: "Bekleyiniz...",
                        result:"formbuilder_gimcqu_submit",
                    });
               });
                if($("#fon-formbuilder_gimcqu .form-check-input.multiple").length > 0){
                    var _requiredCheckboxes = $("#fon-formbuilder_gimcqu .form-check-input.multiple:checkbox[required]");
                    _requiredCheckboxes.each(function (i, el) {
                      var _checkboxList = $(this).closest(".fon-formbuilder-checkbox-content");
                
                      if (!_checkboxList.hasClass("rqCheckboxList")) {
                        _checkboxList.addClass("rqCheckboxList");
                      }
                    });
                
                    var _requiredCheckboxLists = $(".rqCheckboxList");
                    
                    _requiredCheckboxLists.each(function (i, el) {
                      var _checkboxList = $(this);
                      _checkboxList.on("change", "input[type=\"checkbox\"]", function (e) {
                        updateCheckboxesRequired($(this).parents(".rqCheckboxList"));
                      });
                
                      updateCheckboxesRequired(_checkboxList);
                    });
                    
                    function updateCheckboxesRequired(_checkboxList) {
                      var _checkbox = _checkboxList.find("input[type=\"checkbox\"]").eq(0),
                        checkboxName = _checkbox.attr("name"),
                        checkboxNameAttr = "[name=\"" + checkboxName + "\"]",
                        _checkBoxes = _checkboxList.find("input[type=\"checkbox\"]" + checkboxNameAttr);
                
                      if (_checkboxList.find(checkboxNameAttr + ":checked").length > 0) {
                        _checkBoxes.prop("required", false);
                      } else {
                        _checkBoxes.prop("required", true);
                      }
                    }
                }
                
                
            });
            
         </script>
         	<script>
        $(document).ready(function() {
            $('.btn-cart').on('click', function() {

                var $btn = $(this);
                var productData = {
                    id:       $btn.data('id'),
                    name:     $btn.data('name'),
                    price:    parseFloat($btn.data('price')),
                    currency: $btn.data('currency') || 'TRY'
                };
                                if (typeof gtag === 'function') {
                    gtag('event', 'add_to_cart', {
                        'currency': productData.currency,
                        'value': productData.price,
                        'items': [{
                            'item_id': productData.id,
                            'item_name': productData.name,
                            'price': productData.price,
                            'quantity': 1
                        }]
                    });
                }
                                            });
        });
	</script>

	<script>
	    var fonGTSelector = "";
	    var fonGTLook = "popup";
	    var fonGTAction = "after";
		var translatorDiv = '<div id="fon-gt-translator"></div>';
		
		if(fonGTSelector) {
			var $el = $(fonGTSelector);
			if ($el.length) {               
                var inheritedDisplay = $el.css("display");
				var inheritedAlign = $el.css("vertical-align");
				var inheritedFloat = $el.css("float");
				var inheritedHeight = $el.outerHeight();
				var newEl = jQuery("<div>", {
					id: "fon-gt-translator-wrapper"
				}).css({
					"display": inheritedFloat !== "none" ? "block" : (inheritedDisplay !== "none" ? inheritedDisplay : "inline-block"),
					"vertical-align": inheritedAlign !== "baseline" ? inheritedAlign : "middle",
					"float": inheritedFloat !== "none" ? inheritedFloat : "none",
					"height": inheritedHeight,
					"line-height": (inheritedHeight - 4) +'px',
				});
                newEl.append(translatorDiv);
                
                if (fonGTAction === "change") {
                    var newClass = $el.attr("class") ? $el.attr("class").replace(/\bdropdown-toggle\b/, "").trim() : "";
				$el.replaceWith(newEl);
				} else if (fonGTAction === "before") {
					$el.before(newEl);
				} else if (fonGTAction === "after") {
					$el.after(newEl);
				}
			} else {
				jQuery("body").append(translatorDiv);
			}
		} else {
	        jQuery("body").append(translatorDiv);
